< Review>
We appreciate everything and everyone here! Due to illness, we were needing to come here to survive. Trader Joes donates all their food items that haven't been sold by a certain date, that doesn't mean its bad!
Use by date=eat at your own risk
Sell by= by law if not sold by a certain date, must be removed or donated
Expired date= means the flavor might not be up to selling standards, not that its not edible.
They offer a shopping cart full of various foods for 5 dollars
You can buy other items super cheap at table.
You receive two boxes of various items, free per signed in at door, per person
Breads are available
They take donations of clothes, shoes, pet food etc...
Everyone is a volunteer and work hard. So be polite to them please.
Parking is great with disabled available.

Thank you to Joyce and volunteers, at our hardest time, you offered a smile, a hug ( pre Covid) and encouraging words.
Please wear masks to enter.<//Review>

<userid>100288036801816945590</userid><name>Bryan D<//name><Time>1465252058623</Time><Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
Looking for a good place for chinese take away? This could be the place. It's tucked away in a half empty strip mall by the Newark mall. But despite it's need of a remodel and some customer service training, it's pretty good. The spicy items aren't too spicy, but aren't bland either. They offer a good amount of food at a decent price. Some of the chicken items use sliced chicken that is so thin I mistook it for chicken skin the first time. The staff isn't the friendliest, but they get the job done. Give them a try and see what you think. It beats the blandness of Panda Express any day.</review>

<rating>5< /rating><Text>All my visits have been very pleasant.<//Text><pictures>None< /pictures><Resp>None< /Resp><gmapID>0x80dcd1d4c125a9f9:0xc5d9cfbb610f2a65<//gmapID></record></dataset><record>
<name>Premal Bhatt<//name>< text>
Usually I do not write reviews for the Doctors particularly for the doctors with super specialists unless something terrible or abnormal things happen.
My Mother-in law, who is 85 Years old, lives with us in Corona. She is healthy and fit to her age and does the routine walking workouts as a ritual. On Dec 6 2018, she completed her morning routine walk and after a bath started complaining about pain her ankle.
Such a sudden swelling and complaint for pain would lead you to believe the sprain or muscle twitching. My younger son, who is into his internal medicine residency, started icing and keep foot elevated to alleviate the pain. Her pain and swelling subsided but not to a great extent.
We decided to consult nearby ortho but being last day of the week no appointment was available. I am patient with Dr Shail Vyas and contacted his office to see if he can accommodate in his busy schedule. We were there right at 4.30 PM just before closing hours of his office.
Dr Shail Vyas asked few questions after physical exam like whether she had a Fever or duration of the pain and other complaints and recommended to have x ray to rule out any bone or muscle issues. But even before getting X rays he opined that it seems something abnormal like infection. I was just starring at him wondering how in the world sudden traumatic swelling has to do with infection????
After getting X rays, he started elaborating on his observation and opinion----It is a staph infection slowly spreading to the body, you need to get a tissue culture, blood screening and MRI and your next stop should be in your area community hospital ER.
He gave us a note describing all of these recommendations and advised to show it to the attending doctor at the hospital ER.
Attending doctor at the hospital ER room, just looked at the ankle and glanced at the note. In a very sarcastic and apprehensive tone he opined that it could a gout or minor hair line crack and why these super specialists would get to a conclusion even without a blood test? After a long wait, Blood work, MRI and haggling 8 hours after her admission attending doctor admitted that it is a staph infection and we must follow the procedure prescribed by Dr Vyas!!!
My mother in-law was diagnosed with staph infection and had to undergo surgery on emergency basis as infection was spreading fast due to weak immune system. She is still undergoing wound care treatment at home.
I cannot imagine if Dr vyas would not have advised us to go to ER as our next stop. I wish majority of doctors and specialist doctors would have such acumen and professional integrity.

Here my experience is contrary to my belief and encouraged me to write a honest review.< /text>

< review>
What a fantastic find! I wasn't planning to make a purchase because I was just looking around but once I started reading the menu I knew I couldn't leave without making a purchase. Good thing too because the food was delightful! I ordered the CA Turkey Love sandwich for myself and the Hot Italian sandwich for my husband. The customer service was great! We ended up eating half for lunch and had the other half for dinner. The sandwiches were nicely toasted open face before the halves were put together. This allowed for the flavors to meld nicely. Every bite of mine made my mouth so happy! If you're in the area I highly recommend stopping by and grabbing a sandwich. I will definitely return for another as well as some of the other delectables they have on their menu.<//review>

<pics>None<//pics>< review>
Last month I stayed there Sunday - Friday two consecutive weeks. I was a guy traveling on business without my family. It was reasonably clean and safe. Right next to the highway and next a reasonably priced grocery store. My first week on the top floor I got a good room. My only problem was that dishes don't come in the room but you ask for them. My first morning I ask and was told they would be delivered that AM. After work I had to ask again and they gave me a pile of dishes and a coffee maker to carry up so I could make dinner.

The breakfast is pretty sparse having granola bars, apples, oranges and oatmeal packets. The problem is most mornings the oatmeal was only regular flavor with nothing but the coffee sweetners to put in it. They had light roast, dark roast and water for tea or hot chocolate. No decaf but I could make it in my room when I had a coffee maker.

The second week I was on the middle floor. Still clean but I could hear every footstep above me and the recliner was broken. As I was checking in on Nov 1st I ask why they were sold out and was told it was Welfare check day and they always fill up that day. As I was unloading my cart I had a guy walking the hotel (rooms open to outdoors) offering to sell me a $10 "new" leather jacket. I almost flashed him my badge but he moved on when I said no.

I did have trouble getting dishes again. I got most the day of check in but was told there were no coffee makes available. Not a huge deal to head back to the police academy the next day with no decaf and got it the next day when I ask.  In this room I also had toilet problems that resulted in being handed a plunger from the desk at first, a visit by mantience the next day and getting to keep the plunger the rest of the week when problems returned.

That week we also had the Internet go out around lunch and it took them about 48hrs to get it up and working. Xfinity came out on that second day. At home when I call Xfinity in the evening they have fixed it that night or in the AM at the latest. I just upped the data on my cell. Cost a few bucks but with the cheap hotel price I was still ahead.

Overall I am rating it 3 stars as it was clean, safe, close to the police academy and cheap. It's no 3, 4 or 5 star hotel experience but it's an inexpensive place to stay. If you want the 4 star hotel you can pay $125/night in that area but I paid $75 with taxes and dealt with these things. I would still go back for the cost savings.<//review>
